행위</span></p>\n\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:40.0pt\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%\">(21) </span><span lang=\"KO\" style=\"font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%\">. </span><span lang=\"KO\" style=\"font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%\">뿐만 아니라</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%\">,
